***сосуд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́д</a> (3532)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">съсудъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sŭsudŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Proto-Slavic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъ-</i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sǫdъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosúd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосуд.html>сосу́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>vessel (container)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> vessel</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосчитать.html>сосчита́ть</a> (11292)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>со-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">so-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сосчитать.html>сосчита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sosčitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сосчи́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to count, to calculate, to compute</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тня</a> (1065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотый.html>со́тый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sótyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sótnja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тен</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a hundred</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a Cossack military unit; company
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>Чёрная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сотня.html>со́тня</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Čórnaja <b>sótnja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Black_Hundreds" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Black Hundreds">Black Hundreds</a></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сотовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товый</a> (13390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соты.html>со́ты</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sóty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sótovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> honeycomb
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товая</a></b> тексту́ра</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sótovaja</b> tekstúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>honeycomb</b> texture</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> telephony</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cell; cellular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́н</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sótovyj</b> telefón</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cellular</b> telephone, mobile phone, <b>cell</b> phone</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sótovyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́тового</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сотовый.html>со́товых</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cellular telephone, mobile phone, cell phone</li></ol>
